        <h2 id="The-Zen-of-Python">The Zen of Python</h2>
<p>From the <a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0020/">PEP 20 -- The Zen of Python</a>:</p>
<blockquote><p>Long time Pythoneer Tim Peters succinctly channels the BDFL's guiding principles for Python's design into 20 aphorisms, only 19 of which have been written down.</p>
</blockquote>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> this
The Zen of Python, by Tim Peters

Beautiful <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span> better than ugly.
Explicit <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span> better than implicit.
Simple <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span> better than complex.
Complex <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span> better than complicated.
Flat <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span> better than nested.
Sparse <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span> better than dense.
Readability counts.
Special cases aren<span class="hljs-string">'t special enough to break the rules.
Although practicality beats purity.
Errors should never pass silently.
Unless explicitly silenced.
In the face of ambiguity, refuse the temptation to guess.
There should be one-- and preferably only one --obvious way to do it.
Although that way may not be obvious at first unless you'</span>re Dutch.
Now <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span> better than never.
Although never <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span> often better than *right* now.
If the implementation <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span> hard to explain, it<span class="hljs-string">'s a bad idea.
If the implementation is easy to explain, it may be a good idea.
Namespaces are one honking great idea -- let'</span>s do more of those!
</code></pre>
<h2 id="Python-Basics">Python Basics</h2>
<h3 id="Math-Operators">Math Operators</h3>
<p>From <strong>Highest</strong> to <strong>Lowest</strong> precedence:</p>
<table>
<thead><tr>
<th>Operators</th>
<th>Operation</th>
<th>Example</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>**</td>
<td>Exponent</td>
<td><code>2 ** 3 = 8</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>%</td>
<td>Modulus/Remainder</td>
<td><code>22 % 8 = 6</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>//</td>
<td>Integer division</td>
<td><code>22 // 8 = 2</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>/</td>
<td>Division</td>
<td><code>22 / 8 = 2.75</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>*</td>
<td>Multiplication</td>
<td><code>3 * 3 = 9</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>-</td>
<td>Subtraction</td>
<td><code>5 - 2 = 3</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>+</td>
<td>Addition</td>
<td><code>2 + 2 = 4</code></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>Examples of expressions in the interactive shell:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-number">2</span> + <span class="hljs-number">3</span> * <span class="hljs-number">6</span>
<span class="hljs-number">20</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>(<span class="hljs-number">2</span> + <span class="hljs-number">3</span>) * <span class="hljs-number">6</span>
<span class="hljs-number">30</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-number">2</span> ** <span class="hljs-number">8</span>
<span class="hljs-number">256</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-number">23</span> // <span class="hljs-number">7</span>
<span class="hljs-number">3</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-number">23</span> % <span class="hljs-number">7</span>
<span class="hljs-number">2</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>(<span class="hljs-number">5</span> - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>) * ((<span class="hljs-number">7</span> + <span class="hljs-number">1</span>) / (<span class="hljs-number">3</span> - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>))
<span class="hljs-number">16.0</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="Data-Types">Data Types</h3>
<table>
<thead><tr>
<th>Data Type</th>
<th>Examples</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Integers</td>
<td><code>-2, -1, 0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Floating-point numbers</td>
<td><code>-1.25, -1.0, --0.5, 0.0, 0.5, 1.0, 1.25</code></td>

</tr>
</tbody>

<h3 id="String-Concatenation-and-Replication">String Concatenation and Replication</h3>
<p>String concatenation:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-string">'Alice'</span> <span class="hljs-string">'Bob'</span>
<span class="hljs-string">'AliceBob'</span>
</code></pre>
<p>Note: Avoid <code>+</code> operator for string concatenation. Prefer string formatting.</p>
<p>String Replication:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-string">'Alice'</span> * <span class="hljs-number">5</span>
<span class="hljs-string">'AliceAliceAliceAliceAlice'</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="Variables">Variables</h3>
<p>You can name a variable anything as long as it obeys the following rules:</p>
<ol>
<li>It can be only one word.</li>
<li>It can use only letters, numbers, and the underscore (<code>_</code>) character.</li>
<li>It can’t begin with a number.</li>
<li>Variable name starting with an underscore (<code>_</code>) are considered as "unuseful`.</li>
</ol>
<p>Example:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam = <span class="hljs-string">'Hello'</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam
<span class="hljs-string">'Hello'</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>_spam = <span class="hljs-string">'Hello'</span>
</code></pre>
<p><code>_spam</code> should not be used again in the code.</p>
<h3 id="Comments">Comments</h3>
<p>Inline comment:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-comment"># This is a comment</span>
</code></pre>
<p>Multiline comment:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-Python hljs"><span class="hljs-comment"># This is a</span>
<span class="hljs-comment"># multiline comment</span>
</code></pre>
<p>Code with a comment:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs">a = <span class="hljs-number">1</span>  <span class="hljs-comment"># initialization</span>
</code></pre>
<p>Please note the two spaces in front of the comment.</p>
<p>Function docstring:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">def</span> <span class="hljs-title">foo</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span>:</span>
    <span class="hljs-string">"""
    This is a function docstring
    You can also use:
    ''' Function Docstring '''
    """</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="The-print()-Function">The print() Function</h3>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>print(<span class="hljs-string">'Hello world!'</span>)
Hello world!
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>a = <span class="hljs-number">1</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>print(<span class="hljs-string">'Hello world!'</span>, a)
Hello world! <span class="hljs-number">1</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="The-input()-Function">The input() Function</h3>
<p>Example Code:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>print(<span class="hljs-string">'What is your name?'</span>)   <span class="hljs-comment"># ask for their name</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>myName = input()
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>print(<span class="hljs-string">'It is good to meet you, {}'</span>.format(myName))
What <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span> your name?
Al
It <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span> good to meet you, Al
</code></pre>
<h3 id="The-len()-Function">The len() Function</h3>
<p>Evaluates to the integer value of the number of characters in a string:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>len(<span class="hljs-string">'hello'</span>)
<span class="hljs-number">5</span>
</code></pre>
<p>Note: test of emptiness of strings, lists, dictionary, etc, should <strong>not</strong> use len, but prefer direct
boolean evaluation.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>a = [<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>]
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> a:
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>    print(<span class="hljs-string">"the list is not empty!"</span>)
</code></pre>
<h3 id="The-str(),-int(),-and-float()-Functions">The str(), int(), and float() Functions</h3>
<p>Integer to String or Float:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>str(<span class="hljs-number">29</span>)
<span class="hljs-string">'29'</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>print(<span class="hljs-string">'I am {} years old.'</span>.format(str(<span class="hljs-number">29</span>)))
I am <span class="hljs-number">29</span> years old.
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>str(<span class="hljs-number">-3.14</span>)
<span class="hljs-string">'-3.14'</span>
</code></pre>
<p>Float to Integer:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>int(<span class="hljs-number">7.7</span>)
<span class="hljs-number">7</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>int(<span class="hljs-number">7.7</span>) + <span class="hljs-number">1</span>
<span class="hljs-number">8</span>
</code></pre>
<h2 id="Flow-Control">Flow Control</h2>
<h3 id="Comparison-Operators">Comparison Operators</h3>
<table>
<thead><tr>
<th>Operator</th>
<th>Meaning</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>==</code></td>
<td>Equal to</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>!=</code></td>
<td>Not equal to</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>&lt;</code></td>
<td>Less than</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>&gt;</code></td>
<td>Greater Than</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>&lt;=</code></td>
<td>Less than or Equal to</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>&gt;=</code></td>
<td>Greater than or Equal to</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>These operators evaluate to True or False depending on the values you give them.</p>
<p>Examples:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-number">42</span> == <span class="hljs-number">42</span>
<span class="hljs-literal">True</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-number">40</span> == <span class="hljs-number">42</span>
<span class="hljs-literal">False</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-string">'hello'</span> == <span class="hljs-string">'hello'</span>
<span class="hljs-literal">True</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-string">'hello'</span> == <span class="hljs-string">'Hello'</span>
<span class="hljs-literal">False</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-string">'dog'</span> != <span class="hljs-string">'cat'</span>
<span class="hljs-literal">True</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-number">42</span> == <span class="hljs-number">42.0</span>
<span class="hljs-literal">True</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-number">42</span> == <span class="hljs-string">'42'</span>
<span class="hljs-literal">False</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="Boolean-evaluation">Boolean evaluation</h3>
<p>Never use <code>==</code> or <code>!=</code> operator to evaluate boolean operation. Use the <code>is</code> or <code>is not</code> operators,
or use implicit boolean evaluation.</p>
<p>NO (even if they are valid Python):</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span> == <span class="hljs-literal">True</span>
<span class="hljs-literal">True</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span> != <span class="hljs-literal">False</span>
<span class="hljs-literal">True</span>
</code></pre>
<p>YES (even if they are valid Python):</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span> <span class="hljs-literal">True</span>
<span class="hljs-literal">True</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">not</span> <span class="hljs-literal">False</span>
<span class="hljs-literal">True</span>
</code></pre>
<p>These statements are equivalent:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-Python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> a <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span> <span class="hljs-literal">True</span>:
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>   <span class="hljs-keyword">pass</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> a <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">not</span> <span class="hljs-literal">False</span>:
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>   <span class="hljs-keyword">pass</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> a:
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>   <span class="hljs-keyword">pass</span>
</code></pre>
<p>And these as well:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-Python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> a <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span> <span class="hljs-literal">False</span>:
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>   <span class="hljs-keyword">pass</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> a <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">not</span> <span class="hljs-literal">True</span>:
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>   <span class="hljs-keyword">pass</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">not</span> a:
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>   <span class="hljs-keyword">pass</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="Boolean-Operators">Boolean Operators</h3>
<p>There are three Boolean operators: and, or, and not.</p>
<p>The <em>and</em> Operator’s <em>Truth</em> Table:</p>
<table>
<thead><tr>
<th>Expression</th>
<th>Evaluates to</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>True and True</code></td>
<td><code>True</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>True and False</code></td>
<td><code>False</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>False and True</code></td>
<td><code>False</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>False and False</code></td>
<td><code>False</code></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>The <em>or</em> Operator’s <em>Truth</em> Table:</p>
<table>
<thead><tr>
<th>Expression</th>
<th>Evaluates to</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>True or True</code></td>
<td><code>True</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>True or False</code></td>
<td><code>True</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>False or True</code></td>
<td><code>True</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>False or False</code></td>
<td><code>False</code></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>The <em>not</em> Operator’s <em>Truth</em> Table:</p>
<table>
<thead><tr>
<th>Expression</th>
<th>Evaluates to</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>not True</code></td>
<td><code>False</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>not False</code></td>
<td><code>True</code></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h3 id="Mixing-Boolean-and-Comparison-Operators">Mixing Boolean and Comparison Operators</h3>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>(<span class="hljs-number">4</span> &lt; <span class="hljs-number">5</span>) <span class="hljs-keyword">and</span> (<span class="hljs-number">5</span> &lt; <span class="hljs-number">6</span>)
<span class="hljs-literal">True</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>(<span class="hljs-number">4</span> &lt; <span class="hljs-number">5</span>) <span class="hljs-keyword">and</span> (<span class="hljs-number">9</span> &lt; <span class="hljs-number">6</span>)
<span class="hljs-literal">False</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>(<span class="hljs-number">1</span> == <span class="hljs-number">2</span>) <span class="hljs-keyword">or</span> (<span class="hljs-number">2</span> == <span class="hljs-number">2</span>)
<span class="hljs-literal">True</span>
</code></pre>
<p>You can also use multiple Boolean operators in an expression, along with the comparison operators:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-number">2</span> + <span class="hljs-number">2</span> == <span class="hljs-number">4</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">and</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">not</span> <span class="hljs-number">2</span> + <span class="hljs-number">2</span> == <span class="hljs-number">5</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">and</span> <span class="hljs-number">2</span> * <span class="hljs-number">2</span> == <span class="hljs-number">2</span> + <span class="hljs-number">2</span>
<span class="hljs-literal">True</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="if-Statements">if Statements</h3>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> name == <span class="hljs-string">'Alice'</span>:
    print(<span class="hljs-string">'Hi, Alice.'</span>)
</code></pre>
<h3 id="else-Statements">else Statements</h3>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs">name = <span class="hljs-string">'Bob'</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> name == <span class="hljs-string">'Alice'</span>:
    print(<span class="hljs-string">'Hi, Alice.'</span>)
<span class="hljs-keyword">else</span>:
    print(<span class="hljs-string">'Hello, stranger.'</span>)
</code></pre>
<h3 id="elif-Statements">elif Statements</h3>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs">name = <span class="hljs-string">'Bob'</span>
age = <span class="hljs-number">5</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> name == <span class="hljs-string">'Alice'</span>:
    print(<span class="hljs-string">'Hi, Alice.'</span>)
<span class="hljs-keyword">elif</span> age &lt; <span class="hljs-number">12</span>:
    print(<span class="hljs-string">'You are not Alice, kiddo.'</span>)
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs">name = <span class="hljs-string">'Bob'</span>
age = <span class="hljs-number">30</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> name == <span class="hljs-string">'Alice'</span>:
    print(<span class="hljs-string">'Hi, Alice.'</span>)
<span class="hljs-keyword">elif</span> age &lt; <span class="hljs-number">12</span>:
    print(<span class="hljs-string">'You are not Alice, kiddo.'</span>)
<span class="hljs-keyword">else</span>:
    print(<span class="hljs-string">'You are neither Alice nor a little kid.'</span>)
</code></pre>
<h3 id="while-Loop-Statements">while Loop Statements</h3>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs">spam = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">while</span> spam &lt; <span class="hljs-number">5</span>:
    print(<span class="hljs-string">'Hello, world.'</span>)
    spam = spam + <span class="hljs-number">1</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="break-Statements">break Statements</h3>
<p>If the execution reaches a break statement, it immediately exits the while loop’s clause:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-keyword">while</span> <span class="hljs-literal">True</span>:
    print(<span class="hljs-string">'Please type your name.'</span>)
    name = input()
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> name == <span class="hljs-string">'your name'</span>:
        <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>
print(<span class="hljs-string">'Thank you!'</span>)
</code></pre>
<h3 id="continue-Statements">continue Statements</h3>
<p>When the program execution reaches a continue statement, the program execution immediately jumps back to the start of the loop.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-keyword">while</span> <span class="hljs-literal">True</span>:
    print(<span class="hljs-string">'Who are you?'</span>)
    name = input()
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> name != <span class="hljs-string">'Joe'</span>:
        <span class="hljs-keyword">continue</span>
    print(<span class="hljs-string">'Hello, Joe. What is the password? (It is a fish.)'</span>)
    password = input()
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> password == <span class="hljs-string">'swordfish'</span>:
        <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>
print(<span class="hljs-string">'Access granted.'</span>)
</code></pre>
<h3 id="for-Loops-and-the-range()-Function">for Loops and the range() Function</h3>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>print(<span class="hljs-string">'My name is'</span>)
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> i <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> range(<span class="hljs-number">5</span>):
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>    print(<span class="hljs-string">'Jimmy Five Times ({})'</span>.format(str(i)))
My name <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span>
Jimmy Five Times (<span class="hljs-number">0</span>)
Jimmy Five Times (<span class="hljs-number">1</span>)
Jimmy Five Times (<span class="hljs-number">2</span>)
Jimmy Five Times (<span class="hljs-number">3</span>)
Jimmy Five Times (<span class="hljs-number">4</span>)
</code></pre>
<p>The <em>range()</em> function can also be called with three arguments. The first two arguments will be the start and stop values, and the third will be the step argument. The step is the amount that the variable is increased by after each iteration.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> i <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> range(<span class="hljs-number">0</span>, <span class="hljs-number">10</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>):
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>   print(i)
<span class="hljs-number">0</span>
<span class="hljs-number">2</span>
<span class="hljs-number">4</span>
<span class="hljs-number">6</span>
<span class="hljs-number">8</span>
</code></pre>
<p>You can even use a negative number for the step argument to make the for loop count down instead of up.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> i <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> range(<span class="hljs-number">5</span>, <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">-1</span>):
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>    print(i)
<span class="hljs-number">5</span>
<span class="hljs-number">4</span>
<span class="hljs-number">3</span>
<span class="hljs-number">2</span>
<span class="hljs-number">1</span>
<span class="hljs-number">0</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="For-else-statement">For else statement</h3>
<p>This allows to specify a statement to execute in case of the full loop has been executed. Only
useful when a <code>break</code> condition can occur in the loop:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> i <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> [<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-number">4</span>, <span class="hljs-number">5</span>]:
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>   <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> i == <span class="hljs-number">3</span>:
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>       <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">else</span>:
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>   print(<span class="hljs-string">"only executed when no item of the list is equal to 3"</span>)
</code></pre>
<h3 id="Importing-Modules">Importing Modules</h3>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> random
<span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> i <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> range(<span class="hljs-number">5</span>):

    response = input()
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> response == <span class="hljs-string">'exit'</span>:

    print(<span class="hljs-string">'You typed {}.'</span>.format(response))

<h2 id="Functions">Functions</h2>

Hello Bob
</code></pre>
<h3 id="Return-Values-and-return-Statements">Return Values and return Statements</h3>
<p>When creating a function using the def statement, you can specify what the return value should be with a return statement. A return statement consists of the following:</p>
<ul>
<li><p>The return keyword.</p>
</li>
<li><p>The value or expression that the function should return.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> random
<span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">def</span> <span class="hljs-title">getAnswer</span><span class="hljs-params">(answerNumber)</span>:</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> answerNumber == <span class="hljs-number">1</span>:
        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-string">'It is certain'</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">elif</span> answerNumber == <span class="hljs-number">2</span>:
        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-string">'It is decidedly so'</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">elif</span> answerNumber == <span class="hljs-number">3</span>:
        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-string">'Yes'</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">elif</span> answerNumber == <span class="hljs-number">4</span>:
        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-string">'Reply hazy try again'</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">elif</span> answerNumber == <span class="hljs-number">5</span>:
        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-string">'Ask again later'</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">elif</span> answerNumber == <span class="hljs-number">6</span>:
        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-string">'Concentrate and ask again'</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">elif</span> answerNumber == <span class="hljs-number">7</span>:
        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-string">'My reply is no'</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">elif</span> answerNumber == <span class="hljs-number">8</span>:
        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-string">'Outlook not so good'</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">elif</span> answerNumber == <span class="hljs-number">9</span>:
        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-string">'Very doubtful'</span>

r = random.randint(<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">9</span>)
fortune = getAnswer(r)
print(fortune)
</code></pre>
<h3 id="The-None-Value">The None Value</h3>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam = print(<span class="hljs-string">'Hello!'</span>)
Hello!
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span> <span class="hljs-literal">None</span>
<span class="hljs-literal">True</span>
</code></pre>
<p>Note: never compare to <code>None</code> with the <code>==</code> operator. Always use <code>is</code>.</p>
<h3 id="Keyword-Arguments-and-print()">Keyword Arguments and print()</h3>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>print(<span class="hljs-string">'Hello'</span>, end=<span class="hljs-string">''</span>)
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>print(<span class="hljs-string">'World'</span>)
HelloWorld
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>print(<span class="hljs-string">'cats'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'dogs'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'mice'</span>)
cats dogs mice
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>print(<span class="hljs-string">'cats'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'dogs'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'mice'</span>, sep=<span class="hljs-string">','</span>)
cats,dogs,mice
</code></pre>
<h3 id="Local-and-Global-Scope">Local and Global Scope</h3>
<ul>
<li><p>Code in the global scope cannot use any local variables.</p>
</li>
<li><p>However, a local scope can access global variables.</p>
</li>
<li><p>Code in a function’s local scope cannot use variables in any other local scope.</p>
</li>
<li><p>You can use the same name for different variables if they are in different scopes. That is, there can be a local variable named spam and a global variable also named spam.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="The-global-Statement">The global Statement</h3>
<p>If you need to modify a global variable from within a function, use the global statement:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">def</span> <span class="hljs-title">spam</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span>:</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>    <span class="hljs-keyword">global</span> eggs
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>    eggs = <span class="hljs-string">'spam'</span>
&gt;&gt;&gt;
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>eggs = <span class="hljs-string">'global'</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam()
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>print(eggs)
spam
</code></pre>
<p>There are four rules to tell whether a variable is in a local scope or global scope:</p>
<ol>
<li><p>If a variable is being used in the global scope (that is, outside of all functions), then it is always a global variable.</p>
</li>
<li><p>If there is a global statement for that variable in a function, it is a global variable.</p>
</li>
<li><p>Otherwise, if the variable is used in an assignment statement in the function, it is a local variable.</p>
</li>
<li><p>But if the variable is not used in an assignment statement, it is a global variable.</p>
</li>
</ol>
<h2 id="Exception-Handling">Exception Handling</h2>
<h3 id="Basic-exception-handling">Basic exception handling</h3>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">def</span> <span class="hljs-title">spam</span><span class="hljs-params">(divideBy)</span>:</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>    <span class="hljs-keyword">try</span>:
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-number">42</span> / divideBy
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>    <span class="hljs-keyword">except</span> ZeroDivisionError <span class="hljs-keyword">as</span> e:
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>        print(<span class="hljs-string">'Error: Invalid argument: {}'</span>.format(e))
&gt;&gt;&gt;
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>print(spam(<span class="hljs-number">2</span>))
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>print(spam(<span class="hljs-number">12</span>))
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>print(spam(<span class="hljs-number">0</span>))
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>print(spam(<span class="hljs-number">1</span>))
<span class="hljs-number">21.0</span>
<span class="hljs-number">3.5</span>
Error: Invalid argument: division by zero
<span class="hljs-literal">None</span>
<span class="hljs-number">42.0</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="Final-code-in-exception-handling">Final code in exception handling</h3>
<p>Code inside the <code>finally</code> section is always executed, no matter if an exception has been raised or
not, and even if an exception is not caught.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">def</span> <span class="hljs-title">spam</span><span class="hljs-params">(divideBy)</span>:</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>    <span class="hljs-keyword">try</span>:
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-number">42</span> / divideBy
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>    <span class="hljs-keyword">except</span> ZeroDivisionError <span class="hljs-keyword">as</span> e:
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>        print(<span class="hljs-string">'Error: Invalid argument: {}'</span>.format(e))
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>    <span class="hljs-keyword">finally</span>:
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>        print(<span class="hljs-string">"-- division finished --"</span>)
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>print(spam(<span class="hljs-number">2</span>))
-- division finished --
<span class="hljs-number">21.0</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>print(spam(<span class="hljs-number">12</span>))
-- division finished --
<span class="hljs-number">3.5</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>print(spam(<span class="hljs-number">0</span>))
Error: Invalid Argument division by zero
-- division finished --
<span class="hljs-literal">None</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>print(spam(<span class="hljs-number">1</span>))
-- division finished --
<span class="hljs-number">42.0</span>
</code></pre>

<h3 id="Using-for-Loops-with-Lists">Using for Loops with Lists</h3>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>supplies = [<span class="hljs-string">'pens'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'staplers'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'flame-throwers'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'binders'</span>]

Index <span class="hljs-number">1</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> supplies <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span>: staplers
Index <span class="hljs-number">2</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> supplies <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span>: flame-throwers
