</code></pre>
<h3 id="Looping-Through-Multiple-Lists-with-zip()">Looping Through Multiple Lists with zip()</h3>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>name = [<span class="hljs-string">'Pete'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'John'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'Elizabeth'</span>]
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>age = [<span class="hljs-number">6</span>, <span class="hljs-number">23</span>, <span class="hljs-number">44</span>]
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> n, a <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> zip(name, age):
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>    print(<span class="hljs-string">'{} is {} years old'</span>.format(n, a))
Pete <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span> <span class="hljs-number">6</span> years old
John <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span> <span class="hljs-number">23</span> years old
Elizabeth <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span> <span class="hljs-number">44</span> years old
</code></pre>
<h3 id="The-in-and-not-in-Operators">The in and not in Operators</h3>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-string">'howdy'</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> [<span class="hljs-string">'hello'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'hi'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'howdy'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'heyas'</span>]
<span class="hljs-literal">True</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam = [<span class="hljs-string">'hello'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'hi'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'howdy'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'heyas'</span>]
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-string">'cat'</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> spam
<span class="hljs-literal">False</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-string">'howdy'</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">not</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> spam
<span class="hljs-literal">False</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-string">'cat'</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">not</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> spam
<span class="hljs-literal">True</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="The-Multiple-Assignment-Trick">The Multiple Assignment Trick</h3>
<p>The multiple assignment trick is a shortcut that lets you assign multiple variables with the values in a list in one line of code. So instead of doing this:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>cat = [<span class="hljs-string">'fat'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'orange'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'loud'</span>]

<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>size = cat[<span class="hljs-number">0</span>]

<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>color = cat[<span class="hljs-number">1</span>]

<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>disposition = cat[<span class="hljs-number">2</span>]
</code></pre>
<p>You could type this line of code:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>cat = [<span class="hljs-string">'fat'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'orange'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'loud'</span>]

<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>size, color, disposition = cat
</code></pre>
<p>The multiple assignment trick can also be used to swap the values in two variables:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>a, b = <span class="hljs-string">'Alice'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'Bob'</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>a, b = b, a
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>print(a)
<span class="hljs-string">'Bob'</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>print(b)
<span class="hljs-string">'Alice'</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="Augmented-Assignment-Operators">Augmented Assignment Operators</h3>
<table>
<thead><tr>
<th>Operator</th>
<th>Equivalent</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>spam += 1</code></td>
<td><code>spam = spam + 1</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>spam -= 1</code></td>
<td><code>spam = spam - 1</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>spam *= 1</code></td>
<td><code>spam = spam * 1</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>spam /= 1</code></td>
<td><code>spam = spam / 1</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>spam %= 1</code></td>
<td><code>spam = spam % 1</code></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>Examples:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam = <span class="hljs-string">'Hello'</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam += <span class="hljs-string">' world!'</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam
<span class="hljs-string">'Hello world!'</span>

<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>bacon = [<span class="hljs-string">'Zophie'</span>]
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>bacon *= <span class="hljs-number">3</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>bacon
[<span class="hljs-string">'Zophie'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'Zophie'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'Zophie'</span>]
</code></pre>
<h3 id="Finding-a-Value-in-a-List-with-the-index()-Method">Finding a Value in a List with the index() Method</h3>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam = [<span class="hljs-string">'Zophie'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'Pooka'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'Fat-tail'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'Pooka'</span>]

<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam.index(<span class="hljs-string">'Pooka'</span>)
<span class="hljs-number">1</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="Adding-Values-to-Lists-with-the-append()-and-insert()-Methods">Adding Values to Lists with the append() and insert() Methods</h3>
<p><strong>append()</strong>:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam = [<span class="hljs-string">'cat'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'dog'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'bat'</span>]

<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam.append(<span class="hljs-string">'moose'</span>)

<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam
[<span class="hljs-string">'cat'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'dog'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'bat'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'moose'</span>]
</code></pre>
<p><strong>insert()</strong>:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam = [<span class="hljs-string">'cat'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'dog'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'bat'</span>]

<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam.insert(<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'chicken'</span>)

<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam
[<span class="hljs-string">'cat'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'chicken'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'dog'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'bat'</span>]
</code></pre>
<h3 id="Removing-Values-from-Lists-with-remove()">Removing Values from Lists with remove()</h3>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam = [<span class="hljs-string">'cat'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'bat'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'rat'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'elephant'</span>]

<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam.remove(<span class="hljs-string">'bat'</span>)

<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam
[<span class="hljs-string">'cat'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'rat'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'elephant'</span>]
</code></pre>
<p>If the value appears multiple times in the list, only the first instance of the value will be removed.</p>
<h3 id="Sorting-the-Values-in-a-List-with-the-sort()-Method">Sorting the Values in a List with the sort() Method</h3>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam = [<span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">5</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3.14</span>, <span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">-7</span>]
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam.sort()
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam
[<span class="hljs-number">-7</span>, <span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3.14</span>, <span class="hljs-number">5</span>]
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam = [<span class="hljs-string">'ants'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'cats'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'dogs'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'badgers'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'elephants'</span>]
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam.sort()
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam
[<span class="hljs-string">'ants'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'badgers'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'cats'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'dogs'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'elephants'</span>]
</code></pre>
<p>You can also pass True for the reverse keyword argument to have sort() sort the values in reverse order:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam.sort(reverse=<span class="hljs-literal">True</span>)
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam
[<span class="hljs-string">'elephants'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'dogs'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'cats'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'badgers'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'ants'</span>]
</code></pre>
<p>If you need to sort the values in regular alphabetical order, pass str. lower for the key keyword argument in the sort() method call:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam = [<span class="hljs-string">'a'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'z'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'A'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'Z'</span>]
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam.sort(key=str.lower)
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam
[<span class="hljs-string">'a'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'A'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'z'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'Z'</span>]
</code></pre>
<p>You can use the built-in function <code>sorted</code> to return a new list:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam = [<span class="hljs-string">'ants'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'cats'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'dogs'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'badgers'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'elephants'</span>]
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>sorted(spam)
[<span class="hljs-string">'ants'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'badgers'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'cats'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'dogs'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'elephants'</span>]
</code></pre>
<h3 id="Tuple-Data-Type">Tuple Data Type</h3>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>eggs = (<span class="hljs-string">'hello'</span>, <span class="hljs-number">42</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0.5</span>)
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>eggs[<span class="hljs-number">0</span>]
<span class="hljs-string">'hello'</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>eggs[<span class="hljs-number">1</span>:<span class="hljs-number">3</span>]
(<span class="hljs-number">42</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0.5</span>)
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>len(eggs)
<span class="hljs-number">3</span>
</code></pre>
<p>The main way that tuples are different from lists is that tuples, like strings, are immutable.</p>
<h3 id="Converting-Types-with-the-list()-and-tuple()-Functions">Converting Types with the list() and tuple() Functions</h3>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>tuple([<span class="hljs-string">'cat'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'dog'</span>, <span class="hljs-number">5</span>])
(<span class="hljs-string">'cat'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'dog'</span>, <span class="hljs-number">5</span>)
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>list((<span class="hljs-string">'cat'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'dog'</span>, <span class="hljs-number">5</span>))
[<span class="hljs-string">'cat'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'dog'</span>, <span class="hljs-number">5</span>]
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>list(<span class="hljs-string">'hello'</span>)
[<span class="hljs-string">'h'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'e'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'l'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'l'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'o'</span>]
</code></pre>
<h2 id="Dictionaries-and-Structuring-Data">Dictionaries and Structuring Data</h2>
<p>Example Dictionary:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs">myCat = {<span class="hljs-string">'size'</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'fat'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'color'</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'gray'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'disposition'</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'loud'</span>}
</code></pre>
<h3 id="The-keys(),-values(),-and-items()-Methods">The keys(), values(), and items() Methods</h3>
<p>values():</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam = {<span class="hljs-string">'color'</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'red'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'age'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>}
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> v <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> spam.values():
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>    print(v)
red
<span class="hljs-number">42</span>
</code></pre>
<p>keys():</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> k <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> spam.keys():
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>    print(k)
color
age
</code></pre>
<p>items():</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> i <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> spam.items():
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>    print(i)
(<span class="hljs-string">'color'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'red'</span>)
(<span class="hljs-string">'age'</span>, <span class="hljs-number">42</span>)
</code></pre>
<p>Using the keys(), values(), and items() methods, a for loop can iterate over the keys, values, or key-value pairs in a dictionary, respectively.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs">
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam = {<span class="hljs-string">'color'</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'red'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'age'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>}
&gt;&gt;&gt;
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> k, v <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> spam.items():
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>    print(<span class="hljs-string">'Key: {} Value: {}'</span>.format(k, str(v)))
Key: age Value: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>
Key: color Value: red
</code></pre>
<h3 id="Checking-Whether-a-Key-or-Value-Exists-in-a-Dictionary">Checking Whether a Key or Value Exists in a Dictionary</h3>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam = {<span class="hljs-string">'name'</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'Zophie'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'age'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">7</span>}
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-string">'name'</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> spam.keys()
<span class="hljs-literal">True</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-string">'Zophie'</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> spam.values()
<span class="hljs-literal">True</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-comment"># You can omit the call to keys() when checking for a key</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-string">'color'</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> spam
<span class="hljs-literal">False</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-string">'color'</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">not</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> spam
<span class="hljs-literal">True</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="The-get()-Method">The get() Method</h3>
<p>Get has two parameters: key and default value if the key did not exist</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>picnic_items = {<span class="hljs-string">'apples'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">5</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'cups'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">2</span>}

<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-string">'I am bringing {} cups.'</span>.format(str(picnic_items.get(<span class="hljs-string">'cups'</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>)))
<span class="hljs-string">'I am bringing 2 cups.'</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-string">'I am bringing {} eggs.'</span>.format(str(picnic_items.get(<span class="hljs-string">'eggs'</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>)))
<span class="hljs-string">'I am bringing 0 eggs.'</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="The-setdefault()-Method">The setdefault() Method</h3>
<p>Let's consider this code:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs">spam = {<span class="hljs-string">'name'</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'Pooka'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'age'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">5</span>}

<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> <span class="hljs-string">'color'</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">not</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> spam:
    spam[<span class="hljs-string">'color'</span>] = <span class="hljs-string">'black'</span>
</code></pre>
<p>Using <code>setdefault</code> we could write the same code more succinctly:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam = {<span class="hljs-string">'name'</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'Pooka'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'age'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">5</span>}
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam.setdefault(<span class="hljs-string">'color'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'black'</span>)
<span class="hljs-string">'black'</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam
{<span class="hljs-string">'color'</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'black'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'age'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">5</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'name'</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'Pooka'</span>}
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam.setdefault(<span class="hljs-string">'color'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'white'</span>)
<span class="hljs-string">'black'</span>
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>spam
{<span class="hljs-string">'color'</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'black'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'age'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">5</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'name'</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'Pooka'</span>}
</code></pre>
<h3 id="Pretty-Printing">Pretty Printing</h3>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> pprint
&gt;&gt;&gt;
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>message = <span class="hljs-string">'It was a bright cold day in April, and the clocks were striking
&gt;&gt;&gt; thirteen.'</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>count = {}
&gt;&gt;&gt;
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> character <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> message:
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>    count.setdefault(character, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>)
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>    count[character] = count[character] + <span class="hljs-number">1</span>
&gt;&gt;&gt;
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>pprint.pprint(count)
{<span class="hljs-string">' '</span>: <span class="hljs-number">13</span>,
 <span class="hljs-string">','</span>: <span class="hljs-number">1</span>,
 <span class="hljs-string">'.'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">1</span>,
 <span class="hljs-string">'A'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">1</span>,
 <span class="hljs-string">'I'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">1</span>,
 <span class="hljs-string">'a'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">4</span>,
 <span class="hljs-string">'b'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">1</span>,
 <span class="hljs-string">'c'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">3</span>,
 <span class="hljs-string">'d'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">3</span>,
 <span class="hljs-string">'e'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">5</span>,
 <span class="hljs-string">'g'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">2</span>,
 <span class="hljs-string">'h'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">3</span>,
 <span class="hljs-string">'i'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">6</span>,
 <span class="hljs-string">'k'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">2</span>,
 <span class="hljs-string">'l'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">3</span>,
 <span class="hljs-string">'n'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">4</span>,
 <span class="hljs-string">'o'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">2</span>,
 <span class="hljs-string">'p'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">1</span>,
 <span class="hljs-string">'r'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">5</span>,
 <span class="hljs-string">'s'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">3</span>,
 <span class="hljs-string">'t'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">6</span>,
 <span class="hljs-string">'w'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">2</span>,
 <span class="hljs-string">'y'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">1</span>}
</code></pre>
<h3 id="Merge-two-dictionaries">Merge two dictionaries</h3>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-comment"># in Python 3.5+:</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>x = {<span class="hljs-string">'a'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'b'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">2</span>}
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>y = {<span class="hljs-string">'b'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'c'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">4</span>}
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>z = {**x, **y}
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>z
{<span class="hljs-string">'c'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">4</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'a'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'b'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">3</span>}

<span class="hljs-comment"># in Python 2.7</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>z = dict(x, **y)
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>z
{<span class="hljs-string">'c'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">4</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'a'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'b'</span>: <span class="hljs-number">3</span>}
</code></pre>
<h2 id="sets">sets</h2>
<p>From the Python 3 <a href="https://docs.python.org/3/tutorial/datastructures.html">documentation</a></p>
<blockquote><p>A set is an unordered collection with no duplicate elements. Basic uses include membership testing and eliminating duplicate entries. Set objects also support mathematical operations like union, intersection, difference, and symmetric difference.</p>
</blockquote>
<h3 id="Initializing-a-set">Initializing a set</h3>
<p>There are two ways to create sets: using curly braces <code>{}</code> and the built-in function <code>set()</code></p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s = {<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>}
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s = set([<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>])
</code></pre>
<p>When creating an empty set, be sure to not use the curly braces <code>{}</code> or you will get an empty dictionary instead.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s = {}
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>type(s)
&lt;<span class="hljs-class"><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> '<span class="hljs-title">dict</span>'&gt;
</span></code></pre>
<h3 id="sets:-unordered-collections-of-unique-elements">sets: unordered collections of unique elements</h3>
<p>A set automatically remove all the duplicate values.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s = {<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-number">4</span>}
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s
{<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-number">4</span>}
</code></pre>
<p>And as an unordered data type, they can't be indexed.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s = {<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>}
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s[<span class="hljs-number">0</span>]
Traceback (most recent call last):
  File <span class="hljs-string">"&lt;stdin&gt;"</span>, line <span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> &lt;module&gt;
TypeError: <span class="hljs-string">'set'</span> object does <span class="hljs-keyword">not</span> support indexing
&gt;&gt;&gt;
</code></pre>
<h3 id="set-add()-and-update()">set add() and update()</h3>
<p>Using the <code>add()</code> method we can add a single element to the set.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s = {<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>}
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s.add(<span class="hljs-number">4</span>)
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s
{<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-number">4</span>}
</code></pre>
<p>And with <code>update()</code>, multiple ones .</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s = {<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>}
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s.update([<span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-number">4</span>, <span class="hljs-number">5</span>, <span class="hljs-number">6</span>])
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s
{<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-number">4</span>, <span class="hljs-number">5</span>, <span class="hljs-number">6</span>}  <span class="hljs-comment"># remember, sets automatically remove duplicates</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="set-remove()-and-discard()">set remove() and discard()</h3>
<p>Both methods will remove an element from the set, but <code>remove()</code> will raise a <code>key error</code> if the value doesn't exist.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s = {<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>}
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s.remove(<span class="hljs-number">3</span>)
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s
{<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>}
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s.remove(<span class="hljs-number">3</span>)
Traceback (most recent call last):
  File <span class="hljs-string">"&lt;stdin&gt;"</span>, line <span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> &lt;module&gt;
KeyError: <span class="hljs-number">3</span>
</code></pre>
<p><code>discard()</code> won't raise any errors.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s = {<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>}
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s.discard(<span class="hljs-number">3</span>)
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s
{<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>}
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s.discard(<span class="hljs-number">3</span>)
&gt;&gt;&gt;
</code></pre>
<h3 id="set-union()">set union()</h3>
<p><code>union()</code> or <code>|</code> will create a new set that contains all the elements from the sets provided.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s1 = {<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>}
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s2 = {<span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-number">4</span>, <span class="hljs-number">5</span>}
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s1.union(s2)  <span class="hljs-comment"># or 's1 | s2'</span>
{<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-number">4</span>, <span class="hljs-number">5</span>}
</code></pre>
<h3 id="set-intersection">set intersection</h3>
<p><code>intersection</code> or <code>&amp;</code> will return a set containing only the elements that are common to all of them.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s1 = {<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>}
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s2 = {<span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-number">4</span>}
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s3 = {<span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-number">4</span>, <span class="hljs-number">5</span>}
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s1.intersection(s2, s3)  <span class="hljs-comment"># or 's1 &amp; s2 &amp; s3'</span>
{<span class="hljs-number">3</span>}
</code></pre>
<h3 id="set-difference">set difference</h3>
<p><code>difference</code> or <code>-</code> will return only the elements that are unique to the first set (invoked set).</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s1 = {<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>}
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s2 = {<span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-number">4</span>}
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s1.difference(s2)  <span class="hljs-comment"># or 's1 - s2'</span>
{<span class="hljs-number">1</span>}
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s2.difference(s1) <span class="hljs-comment"># or 's2 - s1'</span>
{<span class="hljs-number">4</span>}
</code></pre>
<h3 id="set-symetric_difference">set symetric_difference</h3>
<p><code>symetric_difference</code> or <code>^</code> will return all the elements that are not common between them.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s1 = {<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>}
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s2 = {<span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-number">4</span>}
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>s1.symmetric_difference(s2)  <span class="hljs-comment"># or 's1 ^ s2'</span>
{<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">4</span>}
</code></pre>
<h2 id="itertools-Module">itertools Module</h2>
<p>The <em>itertools</em> module is a collection of tools intended to be fast and use memory efficiently when handling iterators (like <a href="#lists">lists</a> or <a href="#dictionaries-and-structuring-data">dictionaries</a>).</p>
<p>From the official <a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/itertools.html">Python 3.x documentation</a>:</p>
<blockquote><p>The module standardizes a core set of fast, memory efficient tools that are useful by themselves or in combination. Together, they form an “iterator algebra” making it possible to construct specialized tools succinctly and efficiently in pure Python.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>The <em>itertools</em> module comes in the standard library and must be imported.</p>
<p>The <a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/operator.html">operator</a> module will also be used. This module is not necessary when using itertools, but needed for some of the examples below.</p>
<h3 id="accumulate()">accumulate()</h3>
<p>Makes an iterator that returns the results of a function.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs">itertools.accumulate(iterable[, func])
</code></pre>
<p>Example:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>data = [<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-number">4</span>, <span class="hljs-number">5</span>]
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>result = itertools.accumulate(data, operator.mul)
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> each <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> result:
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>   print(each)
<span class="hljs-number">1</span>
<span class="hljs-number">2</span>
<span class="hljs-number">6</span>
<span class="hljs-number">24</span>
<span class="hljs-number">120</span>
</code></pre>
<p>The operator.mul takes two numbers and multiplies them:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs">operator.mul(<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>)
<span class="hljs-number">2</span>
operator.mul(<span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>)
<span class="hljs-number">6</span>
operator.mul(<span class="hljs-number">6</span>, <span class="hljs-number">4</span>)
<span class="hljs-number">24</span>
operator.mul(<span class="hljs-number">24</span>, <span class="hljs-number">5</span>)
<span class="hljs-number">120</span>
</code></pre>
<p>Passing a function is optional:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>data = [<span class="hljs-number">5</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">6</span>, <span class="hljs-number">4</span>, <span class="hljs-number">5</span>, <span class="hljs-number">9</span>, <span class="hljs-number">1</span>]
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>result = itertools.accumulate(data)
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> each <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> result:
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>   print(each)
<span class="hljs-number">5</span>
<span class="hljs-number">7</span>
<span class="hljs-number">13</span>
<span class="hljs-number">17</span>
<span class="hljs-number">22</span>
<span class="hljs-number">31</span>
<span class="hljs-number">32</span>
</code></pre>
<p>If no function is designated the items will be summed:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-number">5</span>
<span class="hljs-number">5</span> + <span class="hljs-number">2</span> = <span class="hljs-number">7</span>
<span class="hljs-number">7</span> + <span class="hljs-number">6</span> = <span class="hljs-number">13</span>
<span class="hljs-number">13</span> + <span class="hljs-number">4</span> = <span class="hljs-number">17</span>
<span class="hljs-number">17</span> + <span class="hljs-number">5</span> = <span class="hljs-number">22</span>
<span class="hljs-number">22</span> + <span class="hljs-number">9</span> = <span class="hljs-number">31</span>
<span class="hljs-number">31</span> + <span class="hljs-number">1</span> = <span class="hljs-number">32</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="combinations()">combinations()</h3>
<p>Takes an iterable and a integer. This will create all the unique combination that have r members.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs">itertools.combinations(iterable, r)
</code></pre>
<p>Example:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>shapes = [<span class="hljs-string">'circle'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'triangle'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'square'</span>,]
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>result = itertools.combinations(shapes, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>)
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> each <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> result:
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>   print(each)
(<span class="hljs-string">'circle'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'triangle'</span>)
(<span class="hljs-string">'circle'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'square'</span>)
(<span class="hljs-string">'triangle'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'square'</span>)
</code></pre>
<h3 id="combinations_with_replacement()">combinations_with_replacement()</h3>
<p>Just like combinations(), but allows individual elements to be repeated more than once.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs">itertools.combinations_with_replacement(iterable, r)
</code></pre>
<p>Example:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>shapes = [<span class="hljs-string">'circle'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'triangle'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'square'</span>]
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>result = itertools.combinations_with_replacement(shapes, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>)
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> each <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> result:
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>   print(each)
(<span class="hljs-string">'circle'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'circle'</span>)
(<span class="hljs-string">'circle'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'triangle'</span>)
(<span class="hljs-string">'circle'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'square'</span>)
(<span class="hljs-string">'triangle'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'triangle'</span>)
(<span class="hljs-string">'triangle'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'square'</span>)
(<span class="hljs-string">'square'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'square'</span>)
</code></pre>
<h3 id="count()">count()</h3>
<p>Makes an iterator that returns evenly spaced values starting with number start.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs">itertools.count(start=<span class="hljs-number">0</span>, step=<span class="hljs-number">1</span>)
</code></pre>
<p>Example:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> i <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> itertools.count(<span class="hljs-number">10</span>,<span class="hljs-number">3</span>):
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>   print(i)
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>   <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> i &gt; <span class="hljs-number">20</span>:
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>       <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>
<span class="hljs-number">10</span>
<span class="hljs-number">13</span>
<span class="hljs-number">16</span>
<span class="hljs-number">19</span>
<span class="hljs-number">22</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="cycle()">cycle()</h3>
<p>This function cycles through an iterator endlessly.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs">itertools.cycle(iterable)
</code></pre>
<p>Example:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>colors = [<span class="hljs-string">'red'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'orange'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'yellow'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'green'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'blue'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'violet'</span>]
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> color <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> itertools.cycle(colors):
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>   print(color)
red
orange
yellow
green
blue
violet
red
orange
</code></pre>
<p>When reached the end of the iterable it start over again from the beginning.</p>
<h3 id="chain()">chain()</h3>
<p>Take a series of iterables and return them as one long iterable.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs">itertools.chain(*iterables)
</code></pre>
<p>Example:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>colors = [<span class="hljs-string">'red'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'orange'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'yellow'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'green'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'blue'</span>]
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>shapes = [<span class="hljs-string">'circle'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'triangle'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'square'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'pentagon'</span>]
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>result = itertools.chain(colors, shapes)
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> each <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> result:
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>   print(each)
red
orange
yellow
green
blue
circle
triangle
square
pentagon
</code></pre>
<h3 id="compress()">compress()</h3>
<p>Filters one iterable with another.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs">itertools.compress(data, selectors)
</code></pre>
<p>Example:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>shapes = [<span class="hljs-string">'circle'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'triangle'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'square'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'pentagon'</span>]
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>selections = [<span class="hljs-literal">True</span>, <span class="hljs-literal">False</span>, <span class="hljs-literal">True</span>, <span class="hljs-literal">False</span>]
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>result = itertools.compress(shapes, selections)
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> each <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> result:
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>   print(each)
circle
square
</code></pre>
<h3 id="dropwhile()">dropwhile()</h3>
<p>Make an iterator that drops elements from the iterable as long as the predicate is true; afterwards, returns every element.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs">itertools.dropwhile(predicate, iterable)
</code></pre>
<p>Example:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>data = [<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-number">4</span>, <span class="hljs-number">5</span>, <span class="hljs-number">6</span>, <span class="hljs-number">7</span>, <span class="hljs-number">8</span>, <span class="hljs-number">9</span>, <span class="hljs-number">10</span>, <span class="hljs-number">1</span>]
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>result = itertools.dropwhile(<span class="hljs-keyword">lambda</span> x: x&lt;<span class="hljs-number">5</span>, data)
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> each <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> result:
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>   print(each)
<span class="hljs-number">5</span>
<span class="hljs-number">6</span>
<span class="hljs-number">7</span>
<span class="hljs-number">8</span>
<span class="hljs-number">9</span>
<span class="hljs-number">10</span>
<span class="hljs-number">1</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="filterfalse()">filterfalse()</h3>
<p>Makes an iterator that filters elements from iterable returning only those for which the predicate is False.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs">itertools.filterfalse(predicate, iterable)
</code></pre>
<p>Example:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>data = [<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-number">4</span>, <span class="hljs-number">5</span>, <span class="hljs-number">6</span>, <span class="hljs-number">7</span>, <span class="hljs-number">8</span>, <span class="hljs-number">9</span>, <span class="hljs-number">10</span>, <span class="hljs-number">1</span>]
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>result = itertools.filterfalse(<span class="hljs-keyword">lambda</span> x: x&lt;<span class="hljs-number">5</span>, data)
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> each <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> result:
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>   print(each)
<span class="hljs-number">5</span>
<span class="hljs-number">6</span>
<span class="hljs-number">7</span>
<span class="hljs-number">8</span>
<span class="hljs-number">9</span>
<span class="hljs-number">10</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="groupby()">groupby()</h3>
<p>Simply put, this function groups things together.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs">itertools.groupby(iterable, key=<span class="hljs-literal">None</span>)
</code></pre>
<p>Example:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>robots = [{
    <span class="hljs-string">'name'</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'blaster'</span>,
    <span class="hljs-string">'faction'</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'autobot'</span>
}, {
    <span class="hljs-string">'name'</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'galvatron'</span>,
    <span class="hljs-string">'faction'</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'decepticon'</span>
}, {
    <span class="hljs-string">'name'</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'jazz'</span>,
    <span class="hljs-string">'faction'</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'autobot'</span>
}, {
    <span class="hljs-string">'name'</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'metroplex'</span>,
    <span class="hljs-string">'faction'</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'autobot'</span>
}, {
    <span class="hljs-string">'name'</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'megatron'</span>,
    <span class="hljs-string">'faction'</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'decepticon'</span>
}, {
    <span class="hljs-string">'name'</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'starcream'</span>,
    <span class="hljs-string">'faction'</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'decepticon'</span>
}]
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> key, group <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> itertools.groupby(robots, key=<span class="hljs-keyword">lambda</span> x: x[<span class="hljs-string">'faction'</span>]):
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>   print(key)
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>   print(list(group))
autobot
[{<span class="hljs-string">'name'</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'blaster'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'faction'</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'autobot'</span>}]
decepticon
[{<span class="hljs-string">'name'</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'galvatron'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'faction'</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'decepticon'</span>}]

</code></pre>
<h3 id="islice()">islice()</h3>
<p>This function is very much like slices. This allows you to cut out a piece of an iterable.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs">itertools.islice(iterable, start, stop[, step])
</code></pre>
<p>Example:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>colors = [<span class="hljs-string">'red'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'orange'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'yellow'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'green'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'blue'</span>,]
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>few_colors = itertools.islice(colors, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>)
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> each <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> few_colors:
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>   print(each)
red
orange
</code></pre>
<h3 id="permutations()">permutations()</h3>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs">itertools.permutations(iterable, r=<span class="hljs-literal">None</span>)

<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>   print(each)
(<span class="hljs-string">'a'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'b'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'c'</span>)

(<span class="hljs-string">'b'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'a'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'c'</span>)
(<span class="hljs-string">'b'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'c'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'a'</span>)
(<span class="hljs-string">'c'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'a'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'b'</span>)

<h3 id="product()">product()</h3>
<p>Creates the cartesian products from a series of iterables.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>num_data = [<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>]
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>alpha_data = [<span class="hljs-string">'a'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'b'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'c'</span>]

<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> each <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> result:
    print(each)
(<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'a'</span>)
(<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'b'</span>)
(<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'c'</span>)
(<span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'a'</span>)
(<span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'b'</span>)
(<span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'c'</span>)
(<span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'a'</span>)
(<span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'b'</span>)
(<span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'c'</span>)
</code></pre>
<h3 id="repeat()">repeat()</h3>
<p>This function will repeat an object over and over again. Unless, there is a times argument.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs">itertools.repeat(object[, times])
</code></pre>
<p>Example:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> i <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> itertools.repeat(<span class="hljs-string">"spam"</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>):
    print(i)
spam
spam
spam
</code></pre>
<h3 id="starmap()">starmap()</h3>
<p>Makes an iterator that computes the function using arguments obtained from the iterable.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs">itertools.starmap(function, iterable)
</code></pre>
<p>Example:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>data = [(<span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">6</span>), (<span class="hljs-number">8</span>, <span class="hljs-number">4</span>), (<span class="hljs-number">7</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>)]
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>result = itertools.starmap(operator.mul, data)
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> each <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> result:
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>   print(each)
<span class="hljs-number">12</span>
<span class="hljs-number">32</span>
<span class="hljs-number">21</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="takewhile()">takewhile()</h3>
<p>The opposite of dropwhile(). Makes an iterator and returns elements from the iterable as long as the predicate is true.</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs">itertools.takewhile(predicate, iterable)
</code></pre>
<p>Example:</p>
<pre><code class="lang-python hljs"><span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>data = [<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-number">4</span>, <span class="hljs-number">5</span>, <span class="hljs-number">6</span>, <span class="hljs-number">7</span>, <span class="hljs-number">8</span>, <span class="hljs-number">9</span>, <span class="hljs-number">10</span>, <span class="hljs-number">1</span>]
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>result = itertools.takewhile(<span class="hljs-keyword">lambda</span> x: x&lt;<span class="hljs-number">5</span>, data)
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> each <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> result:
<span class="hljs-meta">&gt;&gt;&gt; </span>   print(each)
<span class="hljs-number">1</span>
<span class="hljs-number">2</span>
<span class="hljs-number">3</span>
<span class="hljs-number">4</span>
</code></pre>
